[Notes]
Input and output Models for ACEX1K devices.

The package for this model is a sample IBIS template.
It does not contain a device pinout. Add the device pinout to match the
package type and the pinout for the particular design.
These models were extracted from HSPICE models. 
All models are preliminary.
Only driver model data is provided in these models.

Models with "3" in their signal name means they have 3.3V vccio.
Models with "2" in their signal name means they have 2.5V vccio.
Models with "S" in their signal name means they have slow slew rate 'on'.
Models with "P" in their signal name means they have PCI clamp diode 'on'.
Models with "sP" in their signal name means they have PCI clamp 
diode and slow slew rate 'on'.

Package model  is a dummy model. Actual package pinout model must
be created by the user for any specific programmed pinout.

COMMENTS:
All models in TYP, MIN, and MAX corners.

Model Conditions:
TYP:          2.5V   and 3.3V   TEMP=25C   Process = TT
MIN: (slow)   2.3V   and 3.0V   TEMP=85C   process = SS
MAX: (fast)   2.7V   and 3.6V   TEMP=0C    process = FF

Models extracted from SPICE simulations Altera SPICE models.
